# [19.0.0](https://github.com/sprucelabsai/mercury-workspace/compare/v18.1.4...v19.0.0) (2021-12-14)

### Breaking Changes

- Removed uneeded behaviors from client, including retaining event contracts between runs and the ability to use a client in "contractless" mode ([c0bafd7](https://github.com/sprucelabsai/mercury-workspace/commit/c0bafd7))
